Mockup looks more like a draft, what inputs we will have on the page, approximately how it will look like, location of components,

---
Using already existing components, the quality of work and design would be much better, it will save our time, life :D, nerves, less debt and less things to support.
What I offer to do:
- use one library with ui-components,
- no need design-system, using only ant components, it would be much more beautiful and easier for us,
if it would be a different kind of application, than maybe we will need design-system, but for current application - I do not see the point.
- configure the theme for ui-components library (colors),
- if we need to make it more beautiful or custom, then change ui-components theme colors and build a custom Templates, this will be more than enough. (edited)

    const loading = useSelector((state: AppState) => state.isLoading)

    useEffect(() => {
        ;(async () => {
            await dispatch(fetchInitialState())
        })()
    }, [isAuthenticated])

    if (isLoading) {
        return <Spinner />
    }

    return isAuthenticated && isLoggedIn() ? <PrivateRoutes loading={loading.isLoading} /> : <PublicRoutes />
}
